<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неустойчивый.html>неусто́йчивый</a> (12702)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устойчивый.html>усто́йчивый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustójčivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустойчивый.html>неусто́йчивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neustójčivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unstable, unsteady, fluctuating, changeable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неустойчивый.html>неусто́йчивая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:погода.html>пого́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neustójčivaja</b> pogóda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">changeable weather</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неустойчивый.html>неусто́йчивая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:температура.html>температу́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neustójčivaja</b> temperatúra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">erratic temperature</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неустойчивый.html>неусто́йчивое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердцебиение.html>сердцебие́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neustójčivoje</b> serdcebijénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">erratic heartbeat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry<span class="ib-comma">,</span> physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> labile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неустойчивый.html>неусто́йчивое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:равновесие.html>равнове́сие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neustójčivoje</b> ravnovésije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">labile/unstable equilibrium</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестабильный.html>нестаби́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nestabílʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаткий.html>ша́ткий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šátkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хрупкий.html>хру́пкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xrúpkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустроенность.html>неустро́енность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neustrójennostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустроенность.html>неустро́енности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустроенность.html>неустро́енности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустроенность.html>неустро́енностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>state of being unsettled</li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустроенный.html>неустро́енный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neustrójennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unsettled</li>
<li>disorderly</li>
<li>unsuccessful, not established (person)</li>
<li>not provided for</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уютный.html>ую́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ujútnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неуютный.html>неую́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neujútnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неую́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неую́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>uncomfortable</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> causing loneliness or longing</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нефтепродукт.html>нефтепроду́кт</a> (26482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нефть.html>нефть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neftʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продукт.html>проду́кт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodúkt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нефтепродукт.html>нефтепроду́кт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nefteprodúkt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нефтепродукт.html>нефтепроду́кта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нефтепродукт.html>нефтепроду́кты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нефтепродукт.html>нефтепроду́ктов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">usually in the plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mineral oil, oil product</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> oil, petroleum

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нефтяной.html>нефтяна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:промышленность.html>промы́шленность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neftjanája</b> promýšlennostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>petroleum</b> industry</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***нехитрый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нехитрый.html>нехи́трый</a> (8272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хитрый.html>хи́трый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xítryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нехитрый.html>нехи́трый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nexítryj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(of a person)</i> simple, unsophisticated, artless, guileless</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> simple, unsophisticated
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нехитрый.html>нехи́трое</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto délo <b>nexítroje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">that's not a difficult thing to do; that's no great achievement</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">simple-minded</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простодушный.html>простоду́шный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prostodúšnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">simple</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просто́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prostój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незамысловатый.html>незамыслова́тый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nezamyslovátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несложный.html>несло́жный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neslóžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:немудреный.html>немудрёный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nemudrjónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цензурный.html>цензу́рный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cenzúrnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нецензурный.html>нецензу́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">necenzúrnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нецензу́рнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нецензу́рней</b>)

<ol><li>obscene, indecent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> contrary to the rules of censorship</li></ol>

***нечаянный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нечаянный.html>неча́янный</a> (17347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаять.html>ча́янный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čájannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечаянный.html>неча́янный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nečájannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unexpected
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нечаянный.html>неча́янная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:встреча.html>встре́ча</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nečájannaja</b> vstréča</i> ― <span class="e-translation">unexpected encounter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>unintentional, accidental
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нечаянный.html>неча́янный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выстрел.html>вы́стрел</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nečájannyj</b> výstrel</i> ― <span class="e-translation">random/accidental shot</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***нечего.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чего</a> (838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чего</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néčevo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>there is nothing to (negative genitive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чего</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>néčevo</b> délatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is nothing for me to do.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>there is no need, (one) need not, (it is) no use
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чего</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жаловаться.html>жа́ловаться</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>néčevo</b> žálovatʹsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stop complaining</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">it is no use complaining</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">не́фиг</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">néfig</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial, rude</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">не́хуй</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">néxuj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">не́хер</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">néxer</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The preceding noun or pronoun is in the dative case; the verb that follows is in the infinitive.</li>
<li>Prepositions are inserted between <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and the form of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чему́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нечестивый.html>нечести́вый</a> (28384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечестивый.html>нечести́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nečestívyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>impious, profane, ungodly, unholy, wicked</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nečístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ота́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-otá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистота.html>нечистота́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nečistotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистота.html>нечистоты́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<ol><li>uncleanness</li>
<li>impurity</li>
<li>defectiveness, sloppiness, inaccuracy</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dishonesty</li>
<li>evilness, diabolicalness</li>
<li>dirt</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нечистота.html>нечистоты</a> (28430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Has the form of the plural of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистота.html>нечистота́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nečistotá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">uncleanness, impurity, dirt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистота.html>нечисто́ты</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nečistóty</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистота.html>нечисто́т</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>sewage, scum, filth, night-soil</li>
<li>impurities</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nečístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечисто.html>нечи́сто</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nečísto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистота.html>нечистота́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nečistotá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***нечистый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стый</a> (28392)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nečístyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>dirty, unclean
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лица</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nečístaja</b> úlica</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dirty street</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>defective, sloppy, inaccurate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nečístaja</b> rabóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sloppy work</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dishonest, morally bankrupt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>Там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вестись.html>ведётся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>игра́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tam vedjótsja <b>nečístaja</b> igrá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A dishonest game is being played there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>impure</li>
<li>evil, diabolical
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nečístaja</b> síla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">evil spirit</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dirty</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">grjáznyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загрязнить.html>загрязнённый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zagrjaznjónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sloppy, defective</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неаккуратный.html>неаккура́тный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neakkurátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">топо́рный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">topórnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dishonest</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">grjáznyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мошенни́ческий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mošenníčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обманный.html>обма́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obmánnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">evil</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потусторонний.html>потусторо́нний</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potustorónnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дьявольский.html>дья́вольский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dʹjávolʹskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nečístyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стого</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечистый.html>нечи́стых</a></b>)

<ol><li>devil</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечисть.html>не́чисть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néčistʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечисть.html>не́чисти</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

***нечто.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нечто.html>нечто</a> (1315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечто.html>не́что</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">néčto</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable, invariable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>something
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничто́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ništo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Only used in nominative and accusative cases, with no oblique declensions.</li>
<li>Unlike other words with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">što</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, e.g. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничто́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ništó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">что́-то</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štó-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ко́е-что́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóje-štó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the letter <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ч</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">č</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is pronounced as expected here.</li>
<li>The term is indeclinable. The inflected forms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чего</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">néčevo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чему</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">néčemu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чем</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">néčem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are related but have a different meaning.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">что́-то</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">štó-to</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ко́е-что́</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kóje-štó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
